<script type="text/javascript">
    (function (window, logging, xAppInfo, Proxy) {
        var xAppInfoKey, createProxyFallback, decorateArguments, proxyHandler, createProxy;

        xAppInfoKey = 'x-app-info';
        logging.data = [logging.data, xAppInfoKey, '\u003d', encodeURIComponent(xAppInfo), '|'].join('');

        decorateArguments = function (args) {
            var argPos = 1;
            if (args.length < 2) {
                return;
            }

            if(args[argPos] instanceof Array) {
              args[argPos].push([xAppInfoKey,'\u003d', encodeURIComponent(xAppInfo)].join(''));
              return;
            }
            args[argPos] = args[argPos] || {};
            args[argPos][xAppInfoKey] = xAppInfo;
        };

        proxyHandler = {
            apply: function (target, self, args) {
                decorateArguments(args);
                return target.apply(self, args);
            }
        };

        createProxyFallback = function (target) {
            return function () {
                var i, args;
                args = new Array(arguments.length);
                for (i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
                    args[i] = arguments[i];
                }
                decorateArguments(args);
                target.apply(this, args);
            };
        };

        createProxy = function (target) {
             if (typeof(Proxy) === 'function') {

                return new Proxy(target, proxyHandler);
            }
            return createProxyFallback(target);
        };

        require('dctk/dctk', function (dctk) {
            dctk.logging.logMessage = createProxy(dctk.logging.logMessage);
            dctk.loggingAdapter.logMessage = createProxy(dctk.loggingAdapter.logMessage);
        });

    })(window, window.dctk.logging = window.dctk.logging || {}, 'expweb,release-2021-03-r1.10277.2344661,us-west-2:expweb', window.Proxy);
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    (function (Promise) {
        var loadPolyfill, onError, onSuccess,
            perceivedInstantOnRoundTripEnabled = false;

        function addPerformanceMarker(marker) {
            if (window.dctk && window.dctk.ewePerformance && (typeof window.dctk.ewePerformance.mark === 'function')) {
                window.dctk.ewePerformance.mark(marker);
            } else if (window.performance && window.performance.mark) {
                window.performance.mark(marker);
            }
        }

        onSuccess = function () {
            function handleSearchResponse(request, resolve, reject) {
                var responseText = request.response || request.responseText,
                        parsedResponse,
                        hasOffers,
                        hasError;

                if (request.status === 200) {
                    try {
                        parsedResponse = JSON.parse(responseText);
                        hasError = parsedResponse.content && parsedResponse.content.errorData && parsedResponse.content.errorData.error;
                    } catch(e) {
                        hasError = true;
                    }

                    hasOffers = parsedResponse.content && parsedResponse.content.index && parsedResponse.content.index.length > 0;

                    if (hasError) {
                        reject(request);
                    } else {
                        resolve(parsedResponse);

                        if (hasOffers) {
                            window.pagingRequest.wasSuccessful = true;
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    reject(request);
                }
            }

            window.pagingRequest = new window.Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                var request = new XMLHttpRequest(),
                        baseUrlSegment,
                        selectedLegIndex,
                        fl = '',
                        ul = '';
                request.open('POST', '/flight/search/');
                request.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json;charset=UTF-8');
                request.timeout = 90000;

                if (perceivedInstantOnRoundTripEnabled) {
                    window.pagingXMLHttpRequest = request;
                }

                request.onload = function () {
                    if (request.status === 200) {
                        addPerformanceMarker('requestLiveOffersSuccess');
                    }
                    handleSearchResponse(request, resolve, reject);
                };
                request.ontimeout = function() {
                    handleSearchResponse(request, resolve, reject);
                };
                request.send('{\"trips\":[{\"departureAirportCode\":\"MDE\",\"arrivalAirportCode\":\"CUN\",\"departureDate\":\"2021-03-21\",\"returnDate\":null}],\"numberOfAdults\":1,\"childAges\":[],\"infantInLap\":[false],\"isRefundableFlight\":false,\"isNonStopFlight\":false,\"airlinePreference\":\"\",\"cabinClass\":\"coach\",\"pageSelectionParameters\":{},\"packageType\":\"f\",\"routeType\":\"OneWay\",\"stubFile\":null}');
            });
            addPerformanceMarker('requestLiveOffers');
                require(['dctk/dctk', 'jquery'], function (dctk, $) {
                    var omnitureJSON = $('#omnitureJSON').text() || '{}';
                    dctk.initOmniture(JSON.parse(omnitureJSON));
                });
        };

        if (Promise !== undefined) {
            onSuccess();
            return;
        }

        onError = function (e) {
            require('dctk/dctk', function (dctk) {
                dctk.logging.logError('Can not load polyfill', e);
            });
        };

        loadPolyfill = function (src, onSuccess, onError) {
            var polyfillScriptTag = document.createElement('script');
            polyfillScriptTag.type = "text\/javascript";
            polyfillScriptTag.onload = onSuccess;
            polyfillScriptTag.onerror = onError;
            document.head.appendChild(polyfillScriptTag);
            polyfillScriptTag.src = src;
        };

        loadPolyfill('//a.travel-assets.com/bundles/expweb/flightUx/flights-promise-polyfill-13fab63e49b62a56fcd118a01211ae4d-min.js', onSuccess, onError);

    })(window.Promise)

    var loadPolyfillOnFSR = function (src, onSuccess, onError) {
        var polyfillScriptTag = document.createElement('script');
        polyfillScriptTag.type = "text\/javascript";
        polyfillScriptTag.onload = onSuccess;
        polyfillScriptTag.onerror = onError;
        document.head.appendChild(polyfillScriptTag);
        polyfillScriptTag.src = src;
    };

    (function(Object) {
        var onError,
            onSuccess;

        onSuccess = function (e) {
            require('dctk/dctk', function (dctk) {
                dctk.logging.logMessage('Successfully loaded Object.assign polyfill');
            });
        };

        onError = function (e) {
            require('dctk/dctk', function (dctk) {
                dctk.logging.logError('Can not load Object.assign polyfill', e);
            });

        maximumPrice: 0,

            typeof affirm.ui.payments.get_estimate;

// Log when uTA is not available
require(['jquery'], function($) {
    $('body').one('focus', "[data-provide=utypeahead]", function() {
        var isUtaReady = false;
        require(["universalTypeahead"], function() {
            isUtaReady = true;
        });
        if (!isUtaReady) {
            require(["dctk/clientLogging"], function(cl) {
                var message = {
                    error: "universalTypeaheadNotReadyOnFocus",
                    message: "universalTypeahead module was not ready when user focused on typeahead input",
                }
                window.isUtaModuleNotReadyOnFocus = true;
                cl.logMessage("UniversalTypeahead", message);
            });
        }
    })
});
</script>
